<div class="seo-content">
<h1><strong>Toyota for Sale Philippines | Toyota Price List Philippines 2018</strong></h1>
<hr />
<p><img src="//static.carmudi.com.ph/B9Jx4VR3hrH-h8YT9FI83R3zj7I=//PH/cms/Toyota_Fortuner_desert.jpg" alt="Toyota Fortuner for sale" title="Toyota Fortuner" style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; border: 2px solid #DDD;" width:300px="" height:200px="" /></p>
<p> </p>
<hr />
<p>Toyota Motor Philippines Corporation was established in 1988 and has quickly climbed up the success ladder to now become the biggest automotive company in the country with 43.9% of the market share as of June 2015, leaving competitors such as <a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/mitsubishi/">Mitsubishi</a> (19.2%), <a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/ford/">Ford</a> (7.9%), <a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/isuzu/">Isuzu</a> (7.7%), and <a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/honda/">Honda</a> (6.6%) way behind in sales. In 1995, Toyota’s 82-hectare industrial complex in Santa Rosa, Laguna was designated as a Special Economic Zone and this further strengthened the automaker’s place at the top spot in the industry.</p>
<p>Ask any Filipino what car brand he knows and he’ll definitely mention “Toyota" first, if not among the first, as the interconnected three-oval logo has become prominent on Philippine streets, from the Northern provinces down to the south. With a line-up of 21 Toyota models and 12 <a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/lexus/">Lexus</a> models, not to mention 47 outlets nationwide, Toyota Motor Philippines is as versatile and accomplished as the in-demand cars that they are manufacturing. If you’re searching for your very own Toyota, whether a van for business or a sedan for daily driving, Carmudi is the best platform for you to shop and get to know the leading Toyota models. Read on and click the links for more information.</p>
<p> </p>
<hr /><div style="background-color: #e0e0e0; margin-left: 20px; margin-right: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 8px; padding-right: 8px; padding-top: 8px;">

<span itemprop="name"><span style="font-size:14px;">Toyota</span></span>

<h2><strong>Toyota Hatchbacks for sale Philippines</strong></h2>
<h2><a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/toyota/wigo/"><strong>Toyota Wigo for sale Philippines</strong></a></h2>
<h3><strong>Toyota Wigo Engine Specs</strong></h3>
<p>Under the hood of the two variants of this practical mini vehicle is the same 1.0-liter DOHC 1KR-FE engine that can either be mated with a four-speed automatic gearbox or five-speed manual gearbox. The complete details of its engine can be found below:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">1.0 L 1KR-FE, 12 valve, DOHC, Electric Fuel Injection engine</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Cylinders: 3-cylinder</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Horsepower: 64.1 hp</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Torque: 85 Nm</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h3><strong>Toyota Wigo Fuel Consumption</strong></h3>
<p>With a 1.0-liter powertrain, the latest Toyota Wigo is perfect for city driving. Here are some of the average fuel economy ratings of Wigo hatchbacks in the past few years:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Wigo 2018: 9.34 L/100km</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Wigo 2017: 9.5 L/100km</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Wigo 2016: 6.5 L/100km</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Wigo 2015: 6.5 L/100km</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<p><strong>What are the Toyota Wigo Standout Features?</strong></p>
<p>Don’t judge the Toyota Wigo by its size alone; you will be surprised. The Wigo may be small, but this little hatchback can carry up to five people inside. Not only that, but there’s an extra room for cargo in the rear, too. You’ll also enjoy some of these notable features of the Wigo:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Folding rear bench seats</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Navi-ready display audio with iPod and video playback</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">SRS airbags</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Anti-lock braking system</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h2><a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/toyota/yaris/"><strong>Toyota Yaris for sale in the Philippines</strong></a></h2>
<h3><strong>Toyota Yaris Engine Specs</strong></h3>
<p>The current Toyota Yaris received new updates from the inside out, and that included under the hood, too. The new Toyota Yaris now sports a 1.5-liter CVT engine and 1.3 E-liter DOHC 16-valve inline four Dual VVT-i, which now gives the Yaris a greater fuel economy. The smaller 1.3-liter 1NR-FE engine can produce an output of 97.6 hp and a 123 Nm of torque. Details on its 1.5-liter engine, on the other hand, can be found below:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Base engine: 1.3L Dual VVT-i 4-cylinder</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Cylinders: 4-cylinder</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Horsepower: 105.5 hp</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Torque: 140 Nm</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h3><strong>Toyota Yaris Fuel Consumption</strong></h3>
<p>The Toyota Yaris gives a good fuel economy rate compared to rivals, thanks to its new Dual VVT-i engines with a Continuously Variable Transmission. Here are some average fuel efficiency rates of Toyota Yaris models from the past few years:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Yaris 2018: 11.2 L/100KM</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Yaris 2017: 6.0 avg L/100KM</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Yaris 2016: 6.0 avg L/100KM</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Yaris 2015: 6.1 avg L/100KM</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h3><strong>What are the Toyota Yaris Standout Features?</strong></h3>
<p>The Toyota Yaris is equipped with a lot of amenities that will deliver an enjoyable, comfortable, and most importantly, a safe ride to its passengers. Some notable features of the Toyota Yaris include:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">60:40 split folding rear seats</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">7-inch touchscreen display audio with CD/MP3, Bluetooth, voice control and mirror link</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">SRS airbags</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota vehicle security system with alarm</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>

<h2><a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/toyota/altis-1/"><strong>Toyota Corolla Altis for sale in the Philippines</strong></a></h2>
<h3><strong>Toyota Corolla Altis Engine Specs</strong></h3>
<p>The 2018 Toyota Altis is offered with a Dual VVT-i, 4-Cylinder In-Line DOHC, 16 Valve with ACIS manual transmission. 1.6-liter and 2.0-liter engine with either a CVT or 6-speed manual transmission. The smaller 1.6-liter 1ZR- FE Dual VVT-I engine delivers an output of 120.3 hp and a 154 Nm of torque. The bigger 2.0-liter 3ZR-FE Dual VVT-I engine, on the other hand, has the following engine specifications:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Base engine: 2.0-liter 3ZR-FE Dual VVT-I engine</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Cylinders: 4-cylinder</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Horsepower: 143 hp</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Torque: 187 Nm</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h3><strong>Toyota Corolla Altis Fuel Consumption</strong></h3>
<p>The Toyota Corolla Altis is impressive in many ways than one, and its fuel economy is one of the things that make it a smart choice for drivers in the Philippines. With a Euro 4-compliant Dual VVT-I engine, the Toyota Corolla Altis gives the following average fuel efficiency rates in the past few years:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Corolla Altis 2018: 10 L/100km</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Corolla Altis 2017: 7.4 avg L/100KM</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Corolla Altis 2016: 7.4 avg L/100KM</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota Corolla Altis 2015: 7.3 avg L/100KM</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h3><strong>What are the Toyota Corolla Altis Standout Features?</strong></h3>
<p>The Toyota Corolla Altis is now more attractive with the facelift it received. Some updates included new chrome accents, lights, and a new front design. But more than that, the new Toyota Corolla Altis also received upgrades on its interior design, technology, and safety features, which included:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Vehicle stability control</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Seven airbags</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">New infotainment system</li>

The appearance of this all-new variant is made even more premium, dynamic and sporty than the regular counterpart. Here are the following specifications of the base model:</p>

</ul>

<h2><a href="https://www.carmudi.com.ph/cars/toyota/rav4/"><strong>Toyota RAV4 for sale in the Philippines</strong></a></h2>
<h3><strong>Toyota RAV4 Engine Specs</strong></h3>
<p>The new Toyota RAV4 can be had in four variants, the 4x2 Premium, 4x4 Premium, 4x2 Active, and 4x2 Active +, with some changes on its designs. However, the engines remain the same. The Toyota RAV4’s heart is still a 2.5-liter Dual VVT-i DOHC engine that’s linked to a 6-speed automatic sequential transmission. Its details are as follows:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Base engine: 2.4 liter Dual VVT-i DOHC engine</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Cylinders: 4-cylinder</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Horsepower: 180 hp</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Torque: 233 Nm</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h3><strong>Toyota RAV4 Fuel Consumption</strong></h3>
<p>Though it sports the same 2.5-liter engine, the new Toyota RAV4 now offers a better fuel economy thanks to its new 17-inch wheels. Check out some of the popular Toyota RAV4 years and their fuel consumption rates:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota RAV4 2018: 11 km/l average rating</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota RAV4 2017: 11.4 km/l average rating</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota RAV4 2016: 12.1 km/l average rating</li>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">Toyota RAV4 2015: 10.3 km/l average rating</li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<h3><strong>What are the Toyota RAV4 Standout Features?</strong></h3>
<p>Aside from the refreshing ‘sport-centric’ update on the new Toyota RAV4’s design, occupants can also look forward to having a more comfortable, enjoyable and safer ride with several upgrades on its interior and safety features. Here are some of the notable features of the new RAV4 in the Philippines:</p>
<ul>
<li style="float: left; width: 50%; text-align: justify;">“Terrain-treading" alloy wheels</li>
